## ## Pyra Voice Website — Full Build & Deploy
### Architecture Lessons Learned ⚠️
1. **Next.js rewrites() CANNOT proxy WebSocket** — only HTTP. Must use custom server with `http-proxy`
2. **Coolify public apps**: `git_repository` must be full URL (`https://github.com/...`), not path
3. **Coolify Dockerfile location**: relative to `base_directory`, not repo root
4. **Coolify env vars**: no `is_build_time` field — just `key`, `value`, `is_preview`
5. **Coolify labels**: gzip middleware can interfere with WebSocket
6. **Separate frontend/backend apps**: causes cross-origin WS issues — combine into one app
7. **HTTP/2 + WebSocket**: curl uses HTTP/2 for HTTPS by default, WS needs HTTP/1.1 upgrade
- Type: episodic/deployment | Importance: 9
- Tags: ["coolify","docker","voice"]
- Entities: Bayra,Coolify,Pyra Voice

## ## PyraStore Bot — Build & Fix Progress
### Bug Fix: Search Tool
- **Problem:** Search tool used `search_suggestions.php` which only matches English titles. Arabic queries like "الكترونيا" returned nothing.
- **Fix:** Rewrote search tool to:
  - Map Arabic category names → English (`الكترونيات` → `electronics`, etc.)
  - Always fetch all products from `products.php` and filter locally
  - Fall back to search_suggestions API if no direct match
  - Show popular products if nothing found
- **Updated via:** PUT `/api/v1/workflows/{id}` (not PATCH — n8n doesn't support PATCH)
- Type: episodic/bugfix | Importance: 9
- Tags: ["n8n","api"]
- Entities: n8n,Bayra

## ## TTS Voice Workflow — الطريقة الصحيحة 🎙️
1. `tts` tool → يولّد الملف الصوتي
2. `message` tool → `filePath` + `asVoice: true` يبعته voice note
3. أرد بـ `NO_REPLY` عشان ما يطلع رد نصي مكرر
- **⚠️ الـ `[[tts]]` tags ما بتشتغل!** بتطلع كنص خام
- **⚠️ الـ `MEDIA:/path` ما بتشتغل!** absolute paths محجوبة أمنياً

## ## Email Cron Fix ✅
- Root cause: `imapflow` was installed in `/tmp` → gets cleaned between cron runs
- Fix: Created persistent script at `/home/node/openclaw/tools/email/check-inbox.mjs` with own `node_modules` at `/home/node/openclaw/tools/email/`
- Cron job payload updated to run the persistent script
- **Lesson:** Never install npm deps in `/tmp` for cron jobs — use persistent workspace paths
- Type: episodic/bugfix | Importance: 9
- Entities: OpenClaw

## ## OpenClaw Web UI Dashboard Fix
- Mohammed reported error: "missing scope: operator.read" on Gateway Dashboard (`72.61.255.111:44301`)
- **Root cause:** `allowInsecureAuth: true` over HTTP → no device pairing possible → scopes always empty `[]`
- The code in `gateway-cli-yral0h0h.js` explicitly clears scopes when no device: `if (!device) { scopes = []; }`
- `gateway.auth.scopes` does NOT exist in config schema — scopes come from device pairing only
- **Fix applied:** Enabled TLS with auto-generated self-signed cert:
  ```json
  {"gateway": {"tls": {"enabled": true, "autoGenerate": true}}}
  ```
- HTTPS confirmed working internally: `curl -sk https://localhost:44301/` returns 200, cert CN=openclaw-gateway
- HTTP no longer works (expected)
- **Current status:** Mohammed getting `disconnected (1006): no reason` — likely browser rejecting self-signed cert before WebSocket connects. Needs to accept the cert warning first by visiting `https://72.61.255.111:44301` in browser and clicking "Advanced → Proceed"
- Waiting for Mohammed's confirmation
- Type: episodic/bugfix | Importance: 9
- Entities: OpenClaw Server,Mohammed

## ## Nodes Architecture
### 1.5 Human-to-AI Handoff (Smart Design!)
```
When Mohammed chats with customer directly:
→ Conversation is stored in Postgres memory
→ When removed from blocklist, AI continues with FULL context
→ Seamless handoff - Agent knows everything that happened
```
This ensures AI never starts from zero when taking over a conversation.
- Type: semantic/fact | Importance: 9
- Tags: ["postgresql"]
- Entities: Mohammed

## ## Technical Lessons 📚
### PostgreSQL
- Views: Cannot change column order with `CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW` → DROP first
- Type: semantic/fact | Importance: 8.5
- Tags: ["postgresql"]
- Entities: Supabase

## ## Technical Lessons 📚
### n8n
- Branches run sequentially NOT parallel
- `$('Node').first()` — node must execute BEFORE reference
- "Could not find property option" = node type/version mismatch
- **92 workflows** (25 active) — catalog في `docs/n8n-workflows-catalog.md`
- Type: semantic/fact | Importance: 8.5
- Tags: ["n8n"]
- Entities: n8n

## ## Elite Life System — Full Analysis 🏥
### PostgreSQL Lesson Learned! 📝
- **Problem:** `CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW` لا يسمح بتغيير أسماء الأعمدة
- **Solution:** `DROP VIEW IF EXISTS ... CASCADE` ثم `CREATE VIEW`
- **Documented in:** TOOLS.md
- Type: episodic/lesson | Importance: 8.5
- Tags: ["postgresql","elitelife"]

## ## PyraStore Bot — Build & Fix Progress
### n8n API Lessons
- `PATCH` method NOT allowed — use `PUT` for workflow updates
- `POST .../activate` and `POST .../deactivate` for workflow state
- PUT requires only: name, nodes, connections, settings, staticData (no extra fields)
- Credential creation: `POST /api/v1/credentials` with type `telegramApi`
- Type: episodic/bugfix | Importance: 8.5
- Tags: ["n8n","telegram","api"]
- Entities: n8n,Bayra

## ## Model Cost Tracking ✅
- All OpenRouter + Google models had `cost: 0` — `/status` couldn't report spending
- Updated via `gateway config.patch` in `models.providers.*.models[].cost`
- Prices: Claude Opus $15/$75, Sonnet $3/$15, GPT-4o $2.50/$10, GPT-4o-mini $0.15/$0.60, Gemini 3 Pro $1.25/$10, Gemini 3 Flash $0.15/$0.60
- **Config lesson:** `cost` goes in `models.providers.*.models[].cost`, NOT in `agents.defaults.models` (schema only allows `alias`, `params`, `streaming` there)
- Type: episodic/lesson | Importance: 8.5
- Entities: Gemini,OpenRouter,Claude Max

## ## Tasheel AI WhatsApp Demo — الإنجازات
### إصلاح الـ Workflow (ليلة 7-8 فبراير)

#### المشكلة الأولى: toolHttpRequest مكسور
- `@n8n/n8n-nodes-langchain.toolHttpRequest` (v1.1) عنده bug على n8n instance محمد
- يعطي "The name of this tool is not a valid alphanumeric string" حتى لو الاسم صحيح
- **الحل:** بدّلنا كل الـ tools لـ `toolCode` (JavaScript) — يعمل `fetch()` مباشرة لـ Supabase
- **5 tools شغالين:** getOrCreateClient, createCase, getClientCases, updateCase, saveDocument

#### المشكلة الثانية: مسار الصور مكسور
- Node قديم "Analyze Image (Gemini)" (code node مفصول) كان يسبب `paired_item_no_connection` error
- **الحل:** حذفنا الـ node القديم + صلحنا Set Image Msg expression

#### المشكلة الثالثة: 3 قدرات ناقصة (محمد اكتشفها)
محمد جرّب الـ bot وشاف:
1. **الصور ما تُقرأ** — الـ bot بيقول "تم الاستلام" بس ما بيحلل الصورة
2. **ما في رفع على Google Drive** — المستندات ما بتتحفظ
3. **ما يقدر يبعث صور/ملفات** — فقط text reply

**الحلول اللي أضفناها:**
1. ✅ Gemini Vision بيحلل كل صورة/مستند
2. ✅ رفع أوتوماتيك على Google Drive folder
3. ✅ Tool جديد `sendMedia` عبر Evolution API

**المسار الجديد:**
```
صورة → Get Image → Analyze (Gemini Vision) → Convert to File → Upload to Drive → Set Image Msg → AI Agent
```

## ## MinIO — محمد سأل واتعلم
- شرحتله الفرق بين MinIO standalone vs Supabase
- MinIO = Object Storage فقط (ملفات)
- Supabase = منصة كاملة (DB + Auth + Storage + API)
- MinIO جزء من Supabase Stack (يشغّل الـ Storage)
- قررنا نستخدم Supabase Storage بدل MinIO مستقل — أبسط

## ## Nodes Architecture
### 1. Entry Point
| Node | Type | Purpose |
|------|------|---------|
| **Webhook** | POST /pyraai | Receives messages from Evolution API |
| **If** | Filter | Checks `fromMe: false` (ignore own messages) |
| **If row does not exist** | DataTable | Blocklist check (WAblockNumber) |
| **If1** | Filter | Checks if headers exist |
- Type: semantic/credential | Importance: 7
- Tags: ["api","evolution-api"]
- Entities: Bayra,Evolution API

## ## Nodes Architecture
### 5. Output
| Node | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| **Send text1** | Send reply via Evolution API (15s delay) |
| **Append row in sheet** | Log conversation to Google Sheets |

---
- Type: semantic/credential | Importance: 7
- Tags: ["api","evolution-api"]
- Entities: Evolution API

## ## # Pyra WhatsApp Workflow — Documentation
**Last Updated:** 2026-02-06
**Workflow ID:** XswCOuU2T3gaExUk
**Name:** PyraWhatsapp_Agent
**Status:** Active ✅

---
- Type: semantic/fact | Importance: 6
- Tags: ["whatsapp"]
- Entities: Bayra

## ## Overview
```
Webhook → Filter → Media Processing → AI Agent → Send Reply → Log
```

---
- Type: semantic/fact | Importance: 6
- Entities: n8n,WhatsApp

## ## Nodes Architecture
### 2. Message Type Router (Switch)
Routes to 5 branches based on message type:
- **Text** → Edit Fields6 → AI Agent
- **Audio** → Voice processing pipeline
- **Image** → Image processing pipeline
- **PDF** → Document processing pipeline
- **Video** → Video processing pipeline
- Type: semantic/infrastructure | Importance: 6
- Tags: ["voice"]
- Entities: n8n

## ## Nodes Architecture
### 3. Media Processing Pipelines

#### Voice Pipeline
```
Get voice → Convert to File (audio/ogg) → Transcribe (OpenAI Whisper) → Edit Fields4 → AI Agent
```

#### Image Pipeline
```
Get Images → Convert to File1 → Upload to Drive + Analyze (Gemini 3 Pro) → Edit Fields5 → Limit2 → AI Agent
```
- Uploads to Google Drive folder: `1-xjfWa8dl6oJog3sHqJS31FpAt5mcJu8`
- Analyzes with Gemini 3 Pro Preview
- Captures image caption if present

#### PDF Pipeline
```
Get PDF → Convert to File2 → Upload pdf → Download file → Analyze document (Gemini) → Edit Fields → Limit1 → AI Agent
```

#### Video Pipeline
```
Get Video → Convert to File3 → Upload video → Download video → Analyze video (Gemini) → Edit video Fields → Limit → AI Agent
```
- Type: semantic/infrastructure | Importance: 6
- Tags: ["voice"]
- Entities: Gemini,n8n

## ## Configuration Details
```yaml
Webhook Path: /pyraai
Message Delay: 15000ms (15 seconds) — INTENTIONAL for natural feel
Available Hours: 11 AM - 7 PM (Sunday OFF)
Timezone: Asia/Dubai
Blocklist Table: WAblockNumber
Human Handoff: Via Email (send lead tool)
```

- Type: semantic/reference | Importance: 6
- Entities: Bayra
